 Alam is that under compulsion people either buy sweets from branded shops for double the price or they fall prey to adulterated sweets

 You can easily check home made sweets or cheese made from cottage cheese and synthetic milk
 kaise karen ghar baithe khoe or doodh kii jaanch
 
 
 - Sweet milk made from synthetic milk, mawa and khoya consists of two main ingredients
 khoe main storch kii to vahi doodh kaa protein content badhaane ke liye uria kii, or donon hi hamaare sehat ke liye hanikaarak hai
 - To check starch and urea, you need a little iodine solution which will be easily found in any chemist shop
 iske alaava aapako chahie paradimethil amino benzaldyhide, iskaa bhi solution aapako chemical shop main mil jayega
 To know whether there is a starch in milk cheese or khoya sweets, in a glass bowl, allow a little cheese or dessert to dissolve completely in lukewarm water
 - jab paneer or khoe kii mithai pani main puri tarah disolve ho jaae to usamen chaar se paanch drop iodine solution mila den yahi prakriya doodh ke saath bhi karen
 After adding iodine, if the color of milk, cheese or khoya dessert solution turns blue, then it is adulterated
 - or agar is mishran kaa rang nahin badalata he to iskaa matlab he ki ye shuddh he
 - Urea is often added to synthetic milk and also found in cheese or khoya made from that milk
 - isko test karne ke liye pehle kii tarah hi paneer yaa khoe kaa garam pani main mishran bana ke usamen kuch drop paradimethil amino benzaldyhide kii mila den- agar isamen uria kii maatra hogi to rang pilaa ho jayega
 This is an easy way to test milk, cheese or khoya sweets this Diwali without having to go round the lab from home

 a three-judge bench headed by Justice Naseer ul Mulk told Attorney General Irfan Qadir that former Prime Minister Geelani was convicted of contempt and sentenced for refusing to act on the Supreme Court's order to reopen corruption cases and sentenced Was given peeth ne apane sankshipt aadesh main kaha ki use ummid he ki nae pradhanmantri court ke aadesh par karrwai karenge
 The judges have asked the Attorney General to consult with the Prime Minister and apprise him of his stand during the next hearing of the case
 agali sunwaayee 12 july ko tay kii gai he
 Ashraf, a close aide of Asif Ali Zardari, head of the ruling Pakistan People's Party, has been appointed Prime Minister in place of Gilani
 gilaani ko avmaananaa kaa doshi tehraae jane ke baad supreme court ne 19 june ko ayogy ghoshit kar diya tha
 Gilani did not accede to the top court's repeated orders to approach Swiss authorities to reopen corruption cases against Zardari, after which he was convicted and given a notional sentence on 26 April
